## 706. assistant

_create_time: 1783424605.378782_

Done. I produced a downloadable static-prework package for urgent/correctness/critical-path Polylogue beads.

[Download the full static-prework ZIP](sandbox:/mnt/data/polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework.zip)

Main files:

[Combined task packets — Markdown](sandbox:/mnt/data/polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework/urgent_correctness_task_packets.md)  
[Task packets — JSONL](sandbox:/mnt/data/polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework/urgent_correctness_task_packets.jsonl)  
[Task packets — JSON](sandbox:/mnt/data/polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework/urgent_correctness_task_packets.json)  
[Task index — CSV](sandbox:/mnt/data/polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework/task_index.csv)  
[Coding-agent master prompt](sandbox:/mnt/data/polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework/coding_agent_master_prompt.md)  
[README](sandbox:/mnt/data/polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework/README.md)

The package contains **29 coding-agent-ready task packets**. Each packet has the bead ID, urgency class, what is probably wrong, source anchors, implementation plan, tests to add, verification commands, likely pitfalls, and the expected end state. I did not apply anything to a live Beads database or patch the source tree; this is a static handoff bundle for agents to implement from.

The most concrete mechanisms I found:

`polylogue-37t.15`: `upsert_assertion` defaults missing status to active, so agent-authored blackboard notes can become active trusted assertions unless the caller remembers to force candidate state. The fix is to make `upsert_assertion` the single choke point: all non-user writes become candidate/non-injected by default, and agents cannot overwrite terminal judged state.

`polylogue-kwsb.1`: the daemon and browser-capture receiver have several security seams: GET dispatch lacks a central Host gate, query-string access tokens are accepted broadly, browser-capture auth can be absent by default, and spool quota policy is not central. The packet turns this into a request-admission middleware and receiver-token/spool-governor task.

`polylogue-8jg9.4` / `polylogue-8jg9.2`: there are two blob cleanup regimes. The safe GC path knows about refs, leases, age, and generations; the doctor/repair orphan cleanup path can still use a direct disk-hash orphan detector. The implementation plan routes all destructive cleanup through the lease-aware GC planner and leaves raw orphan detection as preview-only.

`polylogue-9e5.28`: the rigor audit currently has the wrong universe: it audits declared contracts, not the full insight/product registry. The packet makes the product registry the iteration source, so missing contracts become explicit uncovered/exempt rows rather than invisible gaps.

`polylogue-9e5.29`: several aggregate/report paths still have the classic “absent evidence rendered as numeric zero” hazard. The plan adds field-level evidence contracts so public numeric fields can distinguish true zero, unknown, not applicable, and uncovered.

`polylogue-cpf.5` / `polylogue-cpf.6`: temporal provenance can be laundered by aggregates and relative-date parsing uses ambient wall-clock time. The packet introduces a clock seam for query parsing and a weakest-source-wins lattice for aggregate timestamps.

`polylogue-f2qv.*`: the token/cost accounting work is split into five realizable tasks: disjoint token-lane normalization, per-model partition-safe rollups, one pricing resolver, separate API-equivalent and subscription-credit accounting, and materializer versioning so stale provider-usage rows self-heal.

`polylogue-83u.*`: missing referenced blobs and attachment acquisition are split into source-tier reference debt versus index-tier unfetched attachments. That avoids treating `blob_hash NULL` attachments as lost bytes when they may simply never have been acquired.

`polylogue-20d.4` and `polylogue-1xc.12`: structured-only queries should not be blocked by FTS readiness, and FTS health needs drift gauges/metamorphic trigger tests rather than only coarse ready/not-ready checks.

I prioritized trust, data-loss, security, evidence honesty, and critical substrate correctness before demos or feature work. Source anchors in the packets refer to the unpacked snapshot paths and line numbers I inspected, so a coding agent should re-open the files before editing in case the working tree has moved.

import json, pathlib, collections, re
items=[]
for line in pathlib.Path('/mnt/data/work/poly/polylogue/polylogue-beads-export.jsonl').read_text().splitlines():
    if not line.strip(): continue
    o=json.loads(line)
    if o.get('_type')=='issue': items.append(o)
print('issues', len(items))
statuses=collections.Counter(o.get('status') for o in items)
print(statuses)
active=[o for o in items if o.get('status') not in ('closed','done')]
print('active', len(active), collections.Counter(o.get('priority') for o in active))
for pr in ['P1','P2']:
    print('\n---',pr)
    for o in active:
        if o.get('priority')==pr:
            print(o.get('id'), o.get('issue_type'), o.get('status'), o.get('title')[:120])

## 789. assistant

_create_time: 1783424918.535682_

bash -lc cat > /mnt/data/build_v2_prework.py <<'PY'
from __future__ import annotations
import json, csv, shutil, textwrap, hashlib
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone

ROOT = Path('/mnt/data')
OUT = ROOT/'polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework_v2'
REPO = ROOT/'work/poly/repo/polylogue'
BEADS = ROOT/'work/poly/polylogue/polylogue-beads-export.jsonl'
V1 = ROOT/'polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework/urgent_correctness_task_packets.json'
DELIVERY = ROOT/'polylogue_beads_upgrade_setup/delivery_manifest.json'

if OUT.exists(): shutil.rmtree(OUT)
(OUT/'packets').mkdir(parents=True)
(OUT/'agents').mkdir()
(OUT/'tables').mkdir()
(OUT/'patches').mkdir()

issues = {}
all_issues=[]
for line in BEADS.read_text().splitlines():
    if not line.strip(): continue
    o=json.loads(line)
    if o.get('_type')=='issue':
        issues[o['id']] = o
        all_issues.append(o)
items = json.loads(DELIVERY.read_text())['items']
item_by_id={i['id']:i for i in items}
v1_packets=json.loads(V1.read_text())

# Normalize existing packets.
packets=[]
def normalize_v1(p, idx):
    ids=[x.strip() for x in p['id'].split('+')]
    return {
        'order': idx,
        'id': p['id'],
        'ids': ids,
        'title': p['title'],
        'priority': p.get('priority',''),
        'lane': p.get('lane',''),
        'release': item_by_id.get(ids[0],{}).get('release','A-trust-floor'),
        'packet_level': 'deep-mechanism-v1-retained',
        'source_confidence': 'code-anchored from first static pass; re-open anchors before editing',
        'why_now': p.get('why_now',''),
        'mechanism_or_design': p.get('static_diagnosis',''),
        'source_anchors': p.get('files_to_touch_or_inspect',[]),
        'implementation_directives': p.get('implementation_plan',[] if isinstance(p.get('implementation_plan'), list) else [p.get('implementation_plan','')]),
        'tests_to_add': p.get('test_plan',[] if isinstance(p.get('test_plan'), list) else [p.get('test_plan','')]),
        'verification_commands': [p.get('verification','')],
        'pitfalls': p.get('pitfalls',[] if isinstance(p.get('pitfalls'), list) else [p.get('pitfalls','')]),
        'depends_on_packets': p.get('depends_on_packets',[]),
        'expected_end_state': 'The invariant described by the bead is enforced by code/tests and surfaced honestly in status/report outputs.',
        'bead_acceptance': ' / '.join(str(issues.get(i,{}).get('acceptance_criteria','')).splitlines())[:1200],
        'v2_addition': 'Retained from v1; integrated into systematic release/wave maps.'
    }
for i,p in enumerate(v1_packets,1): packets.append(normalize_v1(p,i))

seen=set()
for p in packets:
    seen.update(p['ids'])

# Helper for new packets.
def add(id, title, lane, release, level, confidence, why, mechanism, anchors, directives, tests, verify, pitfalls, deps=None, end=None):
    o=issues.get(id,{})
    order=len(packets)+1
    packets.append({
        'order': order,
        'id': id,
        'ids': [id],
        'title': title,
        'priority': f"P{o.get('priority')}" if o.get('priority') else item_by_id.get(id,{}).get('priority',''),
        'lane': lane,
        'release': release,
        'packet_level': level,
        'source_confidence': confidence,
        'why_now': why,
        'mechanism_or_design': mechanism,
        'source_anchors': anchors,
        'implementation_directives': directives,
        'tests_to_add': tests,
        'verification_commands': verify,
        'pitfalls': pitfalls,
        'depends_on_packets': deps or [],
        'expected_end_state': end or 'The bead has an implementation-ready invariant, patch route, tests, and verification path.',
        'bead_acceptance': ' / '.join(str(o.get('acceptance_criteria','')).splitlines())[:1800],
        'bead_design_excerpt': ' / '.join(str(o.get('design','')).splitlines())[:1800],
        'v2_addition': 'new-v2'
    })

# Add epic/gate pseudo-packets for all P1 epics not deep-coded; they close when children close.
for eid in ['polylogue-s7ae','polylogue-4smp','polylogue-3tl','polylogue-1xc','polylogue-4ts','polylogue-83u']:
    if eid not in seen and eid not in {p['id'] for p in packets} and eid in issues:
        o=issues[eid]
        add(eid, f"Epic closure gate: {o.get('title')}", item_by_id.get(eid,{}).get('lane','epic-gate'), item_by_id.get(eid,{}).get('release',''), 'epic-closure-gate', 'bead metadata only; not a code packet', 'Parent epics should not be coded directly or closed before child proof artifacts exist.', 'Treat this as a closure checklist over child beads, not a direct implementation task.', ['bead export parent/child relationships', 'delivery_manifest release/lane mapping'], ['List open children.', 'Verify each child proof artifact.', 'Run release gate for the epic lane.', 'Close or split remaining children explicitly before closing parent.'], ['Epic gate test/report lists zero unclosed required children.'], ['bd show <epic> --json', 'devtools verify relevant lane'], ['Do not close because “main idea landed.”'])

# Generate coverage tables.
packet_id_set=set()
for p in packets:
    packet_id_set.add(p['id'])
    packet_id_set.update(p['ids'])
active=[o for o in all_issues if o.get('status')!='closed']
critical_active=[]
for o in active:
    di=item_by_id.get(o['id'],{})
    crit=False
    if o.get('priority') in (1,2): crit=True
    if di.get('security_impact') or di.get('data_loss_impact') or di.get('migration_impact') or di.get('public_claim_impact'): crit=True
    if di.get('release') in {'A-trust-floor','B-storage-rebuild-bytes','C-read-evidence-contract','D-agent-context-coordination'}: crit=True
    if crit: critical_active.append(o)

with (OUT/'tables/coverage_matrix.csv').open('w', newline='') as f:
    w=csv.writer(f)
    w.writerow(['id','priority','type','status','release','lane','covered_by_v2_packet','packet_level','title'])
    pmap={}
    for p in packets:
        for i in p['ids']: pmap[i]=p
        pmap[p['id']]=p
    for o in sorted(critical_active, key=lambda x:(x.get('priority') or 9, item_by_id.get(x['id'],{}).get('order',9999), x['id'])):
        p=pmap.get(o['id'])
        w.writerow([o['id'], o.get('priority'), o.get('issue_type'), o.get('status'), item_by_id.get(o['id'],{}).get('release',''), item_by_id.get(o['id'],{}).get('lane',''), bool(p), p.get('packet_level','') if p else '', o.get('title')])

# Source anchor index.
with (OUT/'tables/source_anchor_index.csv').open('w', newline='') as f:
    w=csv.writer(f)
    w.writerow(['packet','anchor'])
    for p in packets:
        for a in p['source_anchors']:
            w.writerow([p['id'], a])

# Dependency waves: packet deps by id.
with (OUT/'tables/task_queue.csv').open('w', newline='') as f:
    w=csv.writer(f)
    w.writerow(['order','packet_id','priority','release','lane','packet_level','depends_on_packets','title'])
    for p in packets:
        w.writerow([p['order'],p['id'],p['priority'],p['release'],p['lane'],p['packet_level'],'; '.join(p['depends_on_packets']),p['title']])

# Write JSON/JSONL.
(OUT/'urgent_correctness_task_packets_v2.json').write_text(json.dumps(packets, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))
with (OUT/'urgent_correctness_task_packets_v2.jsonl').open('w') as f:
    for p in packets: f.write(json.dumps(p, ensure_ascii=False)+'\n')

# Markdown helpers.
def md_list(items, indent=''):
    if not items: return indent+'- (none)\n'
    out=''
    if isinstance(items,str): items=[items]
    for item in items:
        if not item: continue
        out += f"{indent}- {item}\n"
    return out or indent+'- (none)\n'

# Individual packet files.
for p in packets:
    safe=p['id'].replace('/','_').replace(' + ','__').replace(' ','_')
    body=f"""# {p['id']} — {p['title']}

Priority: {p['priority']}  
Release: {p['release']}  
Lane: {p['lane']}  
Packet level: {p['packet_level']}  
Source confidence: {p['source_confidence']}

## Why now

{p['why_now']}

## Mechanism / design diagnosis

{p['mechanism_or_design']}

## Source anchors to reopen before editing

{md_list(p['source_anchors'])}
## Implementation directives

{md_list(p['implementation_directives'])}
## Tests to add

{md_list(p['tests_to_add'])}
## Verification commands

{md_list(p['verification_commands'])}
## Pitfalls

{md_list(p['pitfalls'])}
## Expected end state

{p['expected_end_state']}

## Bead acceptance criteria excerpt

{p.get('bead_acceptance') or '(none captured)'}
"""
    (OUT/'packets'/f"{p['order']:03d}-{safe}.md").write_text(body)

# Combined Markdown.
summary_counts={
    'packet_count': len(packets),
    'v1_retained': sum(1 for p in packets if p['packet_level'].startswith('deep-mechanism-v1')),
    'new_v2': sum(1 for p in packets if p.get('v2_addition')=='new-v2'),
    'critical_active_count': len(critical_active),
    'critical_covered_count': sum(1 for o in critical_active if o['id'] in packet_id_set),
}
intro=f"""# Polylogue urgent/correctness/critical-path static prework v2

Generated: {datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()}

This is a second-pass static handoff bundle. It keeps the first-pass deep bug packets, adds uncovered critical-path beads, and makes the work more systematic: selection rules, coverage matrix, source-anchor index, dependency-aware queue, and per-packet coding instructions.

## Counts

- Packets: {summary_counts['packet_count']}
- V1 packets retained: {summary_counts['v1_retained']}
- New v2 packets: {summary_counts['new_v2']}
- Active critical/correctness/critical-path beads considered by the rule: {summary_counts['critical_active_count']}
- Covered by a v2 packet directly: {summary_counts['critical_covered_count']}

## Selection rule

A bead is treated as critical-path if it is active and any of these are true: priority P1/P2; security/data-loss/migration/public-claim impact in the delivery manifest; or release assignment in trust-floor, storage/rebuild/bytes, read/evidence contract, or agent-context/coordination.

Coverage is not the same as implementation. A covered bead has enough static prework to hand to a coding agent: invariant, source anchors, implementation directives, tests, verification, and pitfalls. Some beads remain covered only by an epic/closure gate or by a lower-depth packet when the right next step is spec/manifest work rather than code.

## Execution doctrine

Start with trust-floor packets, then storage/rebuild, then read/evidence contracts, then agent context/coordination, then variants/lineage/live surfaces. Do not build web/analytics/public claims on top of missing evidence semantics. Do not let agents inject context or write trusted memory before the write-safety and scheduler packets pass.

"""
combined=intro
for p in packets:
    combined += f"\n---\n\n# {p['order']:03d}. {p['id']} — {p['title']}\n\n"
    combined += f"Priority: {p['priority']} | Release: {p['release']} | Lane: {p['lane']} | Level: {p['packet_level']}\n\n"
    combined += f"## Why now\n\n{p['why_now']}\n\n## Mechanism / design\n\n{p['mechanism_or_design']}\n\n## Source anchors\n\n{md_list(p['source_anchors'])}\n## Implementation directives\n\n{md_list(p['implementation_directives'])}\n## Tests\n\n{md_list(p['tests_to_add'])}\n## Verification\n\n{md_list(p['verification_commands'])}\n## Pitfalls\n\n{md_list(p['pitfalls'])}\n"
(OUT/'urgent_correctness_task_packets_v2.md').write_text(combined)

# Systematic reports.
coverage_rows=[]
pmap={}
for p in packets:
    for i in p['ids']: pmap[i]=p
for o in critical_active:
    p=pmap.get(o['id'])
    coverage_rows.append((o,p))
missing=[o for o,p in coverage_rows if not p]
missing_by_release={}
for o in missing:
    missing_by_release.setdefault(item_by_id.get(o['id'],{}).get('release','unknown'),[]).append(o)

report="# Static prework v2 systematic review\n\n"
report += "## What changed from v1\n\n"
report += "V1 was strong on 29 urgent correctness bugs. V2 keeps those and adds the missing critical-path scaffolding around them: blue-green rebuild, bulk ingest, read-contract convergence, ObjectRef/query/finding/citation identity, evidence baskets, claims ledger, context scheduler, judgment queue, work-event write leg, hook/OTLP materialization, coordination proof, variants, compaction recovery, live push/cache/SLO, OriginSpec, and substrate hygiene bugs.\n\n"
report += "## Coverage gaps still deliberately left\n\n"
if missing:
    report += f"{len(missing)} critical-rule beads do not have direct packets yet. Most are lower-depth P2/P3 features in lanes where implementing siblings first will change details. They are listed in `tables/coverage_matrix.csv`.\n\n"
    for rel, arr in sorted(missing_by_release.items(), key=lambda x:(x[0])):
        report += f"### {rel}\n"
        for o in arr[:30]:
            report += f"- {o['id']} P{o.get('priority')} — {o.get('title')}\n"
        if len(arr)>30: report += f"- ... {len(arr)-30} more\n"
else:
    report += "No missing direct packet under the critical-rule selection.\n"
report += "\n## How to use this with coding agents\n\nGive one packet file to one coding agent. Require it to reopen every source anchor, restate the invariant, implement the smallest patch satisfying the tests, run the verification commands, and update the bead with the proof artifact. If source has moved, the agent must re-anchor before editing.\n"
(OUT/'systematic_review.md').write_text(report)

playbook=f"""# Coding-agent master prompt v2

You are implementing one Polylogue Beads packet from `polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework_v2/packets/`.

Rules:

1. Reopen every source anchor before editing. Treat line numbers as snapshot anchors, not as truth after the tree moves.
2. Restate the invariant in your own words before coding.
3. Make the smallest patch that enforces the invariant through one shared chokepoint where the packet asks for one.
4. Add the tests named in the packet. If the exact test file differs, create the nearest focused unit/integration test and explain why.
5. Run the verification commands or the nearest available lane. Preserve command output in the final handoff.
6. Do not close parent epics directly. Close or update only the bead you implemented, plus child follow-ups discovered by tests.
7. Do not turn unknown/absent evidence into zero, empty, green, or success.
8. Do not let non-user agent writes become trusted/injected state unless a packet explicitly says a user judgment happened.
9. Do not publish public claims without claims-ledger/evidence-ref support.

Expected handoff:

- Files changed.
- Invariant enforced.
- Tests added.
- Verification commands and results.
- Any source anchors that moved.
- Follow-up beads if the packet exposed adjacent defects.
"""
(OUT/'agents/coding_agent_master_prompt_v2.md').write_text(playbook)

# Release wave map markdown.
waves={}
for p in packets:
    waves.setdefault(p['release'],[]).append(p)
wave_md="# Packet release/wave map\n\n"
order_release=['A-trust-floor','B-storage-rebuild-bytes','C-read-evidence-contract','D-agent-context-coordination','E-variants-preferences','F-lineage-compaction','G-live-performance','H-web-cockpit','K-interop-origin-export','L-external-legibility','M-substrate-consolidation']
for rel in order_release + [r for r in sorted(waves) if r not in order_release]:
    if rel not in waves: continue
    wave_md += f"## {rel}\n\n"
    for p in sorted(waves[rel], key=lambda x:x['order']):
        deps=', '.join(p['depends_on_packets']) or 'none'
        wave_md += f"- {p['order']:03d}. `{p['id']}` — {p['title']} (deps: {deps})\n"
    wave_md += "\n"
(OUT/'release_wave_map.md').write_text(wave_md)

# Patch manifest for beads: notes/labels to add, not live application.
patch={
    'generated_at': datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
    'source': 'static prework v2',
    'packet_count': len(packets),
    'suggested_labels': {},
    'suggested_notes': {},
}
for p in packets:
    for bid in p['ids']:
        if bid in issues:
            patch['suggested_labels'].setdefault(bid,[]).extend([f"prework:v2", f"lane:{p['lane']}", f"release:{p['release']}", f"packet-level:{p['packet_level']}"])
            patch['suggested_notes'][bid]=f"Static prework v2 packet `{p['id']}` exists: invariant/source anchors/tests/verification in `packets/{p['order']:03d}-...md`."
(OUT/'patches/beads_prework_v2_patch_manifest.json').write_text(json.dumps(patch, indent=2))

# README
readme=f"""# Polylogue urgent/correctness/critical-path static prework v2

This package is a systematic iteration of the first static-prework bundle.

Important files:

- `urgent_correctness_task_packets_v2.md` — all packets in one document.
- `packets/` — one coding-agent-ready Markdown file per packet.
- `urgent_correctness_task_packets_v2.jsonl` — machine-readable queue.
- `tables/task_queue.csv` — compact execution queue.
- `tables/coverage_matrix.csv` — active critical-rule bead coverage.
- `tables/source_anchor_index.csv` — source-anchor lookup by packet.
- `release_wave_map.md` — dependency-aware release grouping.
- `systematic_review.md` — what changed, remaining gaps, and usage notes.
- `agents/coding_agent_master_prompt_v2.md` — prompt to paste before giving an agent one packet.
- `patches/beads_prework_v2_patch_manifest.json` — optional Beads notes/labels patch manifest; not applied live.

The package does not patch Polylogue source and does not mutate a live Beads database.
"""
(OUT/'README.md').write_text(readme)

# Simple SHA manifest.
sha=[]
for p in sorted(OUT.rglob('*')):
    if p.is_file():
        sha.append({'path': str(p.relative_to(OUT)), 'sha256': hashlib.sha256(p.read_bytes()).hexdigest(), 'bytes': p.stat().st_size})
(OUT/'SHA256SUMS.json').write_text(json.dumps(sha, indent=2))

zip_path=ROOT/'polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework_v2.zip'
if zip_path.exists(): zip_path.unlink()
shutil.make_archive(str(zip_path.with_suffix('')), 'zip', OUT)
print(zip_path)
print(json.dumps(summary_counts, indent=2))

## 811. assistant

_create_time: 1783426062.125098_

Done. I rebuilt the static-prework package as a systematic v2 pass over the current Polylogue snapshot.

[Download the systematic v2 ZIP](sandbox:/mnt/data/polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework_v2.zip)

The main entry points are:

[Systematic triage report](sandbox:/mnt/data/polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework_v2/systematic_triage.md)  
[All task packets combined](sandbox:/mnt/data/polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework_v2/urgent_correctness_task_packets_v2.md)  
[Task index CSV](sandbox:/mnt/data/polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework_v2/task_index.csv)  
[Triage matrix CSV](sandbox:/mnt/data/polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework_v2/triage_matrix.csv)  
[Source anchor index](sandbox:/mnt/data/polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework_v2/source_anchor_index.md)  
[Critical-path execution order](sandbox:/mnt/data/polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework_v2/critical_path_execution_order.md)  
[Verification lanes](sandbox:/mnt/data/polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework_v2/verification_lanes.md)  
[Packet quality audit](sandbox:/mnt/data/polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework_v2/packet_quality_audit.md)  
[Coding-agent master prompt v2](sandbox:/mnt/data/polylogue_urgent_bead_static_prework_v2/coding_agent_master_prompt_v2.md)

This version is substantially broader than the first package. The first pass had 29 packets. This one has 194 packetized beads, plus a triage matrix for all 397 active beads. It includes all active P1 beads and the critical/high-value P2 layer, then selected P3/P4 items where they sit on the critical path for demos, contracts, evidence, coordination, or public claims.

I also rebased the source anchors onto the newer Polylogue snapshot instead of the older work directory. The package records the source snapshot, Beads export, git commit, active priority counts, and derived readiness/urgency fields so a coding agent can tell whether a packet is source-localized, bead-localized, epic-level, or still specification-heavy.

The most concrete refined mechanisms include:

`polylogue-37t.15`: the assertion write path needs a real non-user safety chokepoint. The packet anchors this on `upsert_assertion`, `upsert_blackboard_note`, and the current default-active behavior, then gives the implementation rule: non-user authors become candidate/non-injected by default and cannot resurrect terminal judged state.

`polylogue-kwsb.1`: daemon and browser-capture admission need central Host/Origin/token/spool policy, not route-local checks. The packet identifies the daemon auth/origin seams and the browser receiver’s permissive no-token/no-origin behavior.

`polylogue-8jg9.4` / `polylogue-8jg9.2`: destructive blob cleanup still has a direct orphan-cleanup path separate from the safer lease/generation/min-age GC planner. The packet turns this into a precise cleanup-routing task.

`polylogue-9e5.28`: rigor audit is using the wrong universe. It must iterate the insight product registry, not only declared rigor contracts, so missing contracts become explicit uncovered/exempt rows.

`polylogue-9e5.29`, `polylogue-cpf.5`, `polylogue-cpf.6`: numeric absence, temporal provenance, and relative-date parsing are treated as one evidence-honesty cluster: no absent evidence as zero, weakest timestamp source must propagate through aggregates, and relative date parsing needs an injected clock.

`polylogue-a7xr.6`: I corrected this during the iteration. It now has concrete duplicate timestamp/date parser anchors across API, MCP, context selection, read views, archive execution, daemon provenance, embedding status payloads, and insight rebuild paths. The task is now a real centralization packet, not a generic cleanup note.

`polylogue-1xc.12` and related FTS packets: v2 records the duplicated FTS DDL/lifecycle surfaces and turns the work into drift gauges, trigger metamorphic tests, and health reporting rather than a vague “fix FTS” task.

`polylogue-4smp` content-variant packets: v2 explicitly treats content variants as mostly missing product substrate, not as something already covered by provider `variant_index` fields. The packet tells the coding agent to build transformed-content objects, refs, nodes, storage, alignment, projection, and review UX on top of existing evidence refs.

`polylogue-b5l` blue-green rebuild: v2 treats this as absent infrastructure with doctrine anchors, not a half-existing implementation. It specifies generation metadata, old-generation serving, atomic readiness swap, write replay/pausing semantics, and partial-ready prevention.

The package is intentionally not a source patch and not a live Beads database migration. It is a handoff bundle for coding agents: read the master prompt, pick the next Release A/B packet, open the listed source anchors, implement, run the packet’s verification lane, and attach the proof artifact back to the bead.
